===== app/(tabs)/index.tsx =====
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { Alert, FlatList, Linking, View, Text, StyleSheet, TextInput, Pressable, Platform } from "react-native";
import { useActivities } from "@/hooks/useActivities";
import { useCustomers } from "@/hooks/useCustomers";
import { useLocalSearchParams, useRouter } from "expo-router";
import { Activity, ActivityType } from "@/types/domain";
import * as Clipboard from "expo-clipboard";
import { showToast } from "@/lib/toast";

const typeLabel: Record<string, string> = {
  order: "Order",
  customer: "Customer",
  price: "Price",
  system: "System",
  inventory: "Inventory",
};

const actionStyleMap: Record<string, string> = {
  created: "created",
  updated: "updated",
  deleted: "deleted",
};

const typeFilters: Array<{ id: "all" | ActivityType; label: string }> = [
  { id: "all", label: "All" },
  { id: "order", label: "Orders" },
  { id: "customer", label: "Customers" },
  { id: "system", label: "Systems" },
  { id: "price", label: "Prices" },
  { id: "inventory", label: "Inventory" },
];

function parseMetadata(metadata?: string | null) {
  if (!metadata) return {};
  return metadata
    .split(";")
    .map((entry) => entry.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .reduce<Record<string, string>>((acc, entry) => {
      const [key, ...rest] = entry.split("=");
      if (!key || rest.length === 0) return acc;
      acc[key.trim()] = rest.join("=").trim();
      return acc;
    }, {});
}

function resolveActivityTarget(activity: Activity) {
  const meta = parseMetadata(activity.metadata);
  const entityId = activity.entity_id ?? (activity.type === "order" ? meta.order : undefined);
  if (activity.type === "customer") {
    const customerId = activity.entity_id ?? activity.customer_id ?? meta.customer;
    if (customerId) return { path: `/customers/${customerId}`, label: "Customer" };
  }
  if (activity.type === "order" && entityId) return { path: `/orders/${entityId}`, label: "Order" };
  if (activity.type === "system" && entityId) return { path: `/systems/${entityId}`, label: "System" };
  if (activity.type === "price") return { path: "/prices", label: "Prices" };
  if (activity.type === "inventory") return { path: "/(tabs)/reports", label: "Reports" };
  return null;
}

export default function ActivityScreen() {
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const [typeFilter, setTypeFilter] = useState<"all" | ActivityType>("all");
  const { data, isLoading, error } = useActivities();
  const customersQuery = useCustomers();
  const customers = customersQuery.data ?? [];
  const params = useLocalSearchParams();
  const router = useRouter();
  const [flash, setFlash] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const param = Array.isArray(params.flash) ? params.flash[0] : params.flash;
    if (!param) return;
    const message =
      param === "order-created"
        ? "Order created"
        : param === "customer-created"
          ? "Customer created"
          : null;
    if (message) {
      setFlash(message);
      router.setParams({ flash: undefined });
    }
  }, [params.flash, router]);

  const customersById = useMemo(() => {
    const map: Record<string, { name: string; phone?: string }> = {};
    customers.forEach((c) => {
      map[c.id] = { name: c.name, phone: c.phone };
    });
    return map;
  }, [customers]);

  const filtered = useMemo(() => {
    const term = search.trim().toLowerCase();
    return (data ?? []).filter((item) => {
      if (typeFilter !== "all" && item.type !== typeFilter) return false;
      if (!term) return true;
      const customerName = item.customer_id ? customersById[item.customer_id]?.name ?? "" : "";
      const haystack = [
        item.description,
        item.metadata ?? "",
        item.action,
        item.type,
        customerName,
      ]
        .join(" ")
        .toLowerCase();
      return haystack.includes(term);
    });
  }, [data, search, typeFilter, customersById]);

  async function handleCopy(value: string) {
    try {
      await Clipboard.setStringAsync(value);
      showToast("Copied");
    } catch {
      Alert.alert("Copy failed", "Could not copy to clipboard.");
    }
  }

  function handleCall(phone?: string) {
    const sanitized = phone?.replace(/[^0-9+]/g, "") ?? "";
    if (!sanitized) {
      Alert.alert("No phone", "This customer has no valid phone number.");
      return;
    }
    Alert.alert("Call customer?", sanitized, [
      { text: "Cancel", style: "cancel" },
      { text: "Call", onPress: () => Linking.openURL(`tel:${sanitized}`) },
    ]);
  }

  return (
    <View style={styles.container}>
      <Text style={styles.title}>Activity</Text>
      {flash && (
        <View style={styles.flash}>
          <Text style={styles.flashText}>{flash}</Text>
          <Pressable onPress={() => setFlash(null)} hitSlop={8}>
            <Text style={styles.flashClose}>x</Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
      )}
      <TextInput
        style={styles.input}
        placeholder="Search activity"
        value={search}
        onChangeText={setSearch}
      />
      <View style={styles.filterRow}>
        {typeFilters.map((filter) => {
          const active = typeFilter === filter.id;
          return (
            <Pressable
              key={filter.id}
              onPress={() => setTypeFilter(filter.id)}
              style={[styles.filterChip, active && styles.filterChipActive]}
            >
              <Text style={[styles.filterText, active && styles.filterTextActive]}>{filter.label}</Text>
            </Pressable>
          );
        })}
      </View>
      <Pressable onPress={() => setSearch("")} style={styles.clearBtn}>
        <Text style={styles.clearText}>Clear</Text>
      </Pressable>
      {isLoading && <Text style={styles.meta}>Loading...</Text>}
      {error && <Text style={styles.error}>Failed to load activity.</Text>}
      <FlatList
        data={filtered}
        keyExtractor={(item) => item.id}
        contentContainerStyle={styles.listContent}
        ItemSeparatorComponent={() => <View style={styles.separator} />}
        ListEmptyComponent={!isLoading ? <Text style={styles.meta}>No activity found.</Text> : null}
        renderItem={({ item }) => {
          const metaItems = item.metadata
            ? item.metadata.split(";").map((entry) => entry.trim()).filter(Boolean)
            : [];
          const actionVariant = actionStyleMap[item.action] ?? "updated";
          const customer = item.customer_id ? customersById[item.customer_id] : undefined;
          const createdAt = new Date(item.created_at);
          const actionStyle =
            actionVariant === "created"
              ? styles.actionCreated
              : actionVariant === "deleted"
                ? styles.actionDeleted
                : styles.actionUpdated;
          const target = resolveActivityTarget(item);
          return (
            <Pressable
              onPress={() => (target ? router.push(target.path) : undefined)}
              disabled={!target}
              style={({ pressed }) => [
                styles.card,
                pressed && target ? styles.cardPressed : null,
                !target ? styles.cardDisabled : null,
              ]}
            >
              <View style={styles.badgeRow}>
                <Text style={styles.badge}>{typeLabel[item.type] ?? "Event"}</Text>
                <Text style={[styles.actionTag, actionStyle]}>{item.action}</Text>
              </View>
              {customer?.name ? (
                <Text style={styles.customerName}>{customer.name}</Text>
              ) : null}
              <Text style={styles.description}>{item.description}</Text>
              {customer?.name ? (
                <View style={styles.quickActions}>
                  <Pressable
                    onPress={(event) => {
                      event.stopPropagation();
                      handleCall(customer.phone);
                    }}
                    style={styles.quickBtn}
                  >
                    <Text style={styles.quickText}>Call</Text>
                  </Pressable>
                  <Pressable
                    onPress={(event) => {
                      event.stopPropagation();
                      router.push(`/orders/new?customerId=${item.customer_id}`);
                    }}
                    style={styles.quickBtn}
                  >
                    <Text style={styles.quickText}>New order</Text>
                  </Pressable>
                </View>
              ) : null}
              {metaItems.length > 0 && (
                <View style={styles.metaDetailRow}>
                  {metaItems.map((entry) => (
                    <Pressable
                      key={entry}
                      onPress={(event) => {
                        event.stopPropagation();
                        handleCopy(entry);
                      }}
                    >
                      <Text style={styles.metaDetail}>{entry.replace("=", ": ")}</Text>
                    </Pressable>
                  ))}
                </View>
              )}
              {target ? <Text style={styles.openHint}>Open {target.label}</Text> : null}
              <Text style={styles.timeLabel}>Date: {createdAt.toLocaleString()}</Text>
            </Pressable>
          );
        }}
      />
    </View>
  );
}

const cardShadow = Platform.select({
  web: { boxShadow: "0px 6px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)" },
  default: {
    shadowColor: "#000",
    shadowOpacity: 0.05,
    shadowRadius: 6,
    shadowOffset: { width: 0, height: 3 },
    elevation: 2,
  },
});

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: {
    flex: 1,
    padding: 20,
    backgroundColor: "#f7f7f8",
  },
  title: {
    fontSize: 26,
    fontWeight: "700",
    marginBottom: 12,
  },
  listContent: {
    gap: 10,
    paddingBottom: 12,
  },
  input: {
    backgroundColor: "#fff",
    borderRadius: 10,
    paddingHorizontal: 12,
    paddingVertical: 10,

    borderColor: "#ccc",

  },

    justifyContent: "space-between",

===== app/(tabs)/reports/index.tsx =====
import { useEffect, useState, useCallback, useMemo } from "react";
import { Alert, FlatList, InputAccessoryView, Keyboard, Modal, Platform, Pressable, StyleSheet, Text, TextInput, View } from "react-native";
import { Ionicons } from "@expo/vector-icons";
import { router, useLocalSearchParams } from "expo-router";
import { useFocusEffect } from "@react-navigation/native";

import { useDailyReports } from "@/hooks/useReports";
import { setAddShortcut } from "@/lib/addShortcut";
import { useOrdersByDay } from "@/hooks/useOrders";
import { useAdjustInventory, useCreateRefill, useInventoryRefills } from "@/hooks/useInventory";
import { useCreateExpense, useDeleteExpense, useExpenses } from "@/hooks/useExpenses";
import { usePriceSettings } from "@/hooks/usePrices";
import { DailyReportRow, InventorySnapshot } from "@/types/domain";

type NormalizedSnapshot = {
  as_of: string;
  reason?: string | null;
  full12: number;
  empty12: number;
  total12: number;
  full48: number;
  empty48: number;
  total48: number;
};

type RefillEntry = {
  timeOfDay: "morning" | "evening";
  buy12: number;
  ret12: number;
  buy48: number;
  ret48: number;
};

type FixEntry = {
  full12: number;
  empty12: number;
  full48: number;
  empty48: number;
  reason: string;
  note?: string;
  delta12: { full: number; empty: number };
  delta48: { full: number; empty: number };
};

export default function ReportsScreen() {
  const { data, isLoading, error, refetch } = useDailyReports();
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<"payments" | "inventory">("payments");
  const [expenseModalOpen, setExpenseModalOpen] = useState(false);
  const [expenseDate, setExpenseDate] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [expenseType, setExpenseType] = useState("fuel");
  const [customExpenseType, setCustomExpenseType] = useState("");
  const [expenseAmount, setExpenseAmount] = useState("");
  const [expenseNote, setExpenseNote] = useState("");
  const [useCustomType, setUseCustomType] = useState(false);
  const createExpense = useCreateExpense();
  const deleteExpense = useDeleteExpense();
  const params = useLocalSearchParams<{ mode?: string; addExpense?: string; expand?: string; date?: string }>();
  const [routeHandled, setRouteHandled] = useState(false);
  const [allowExpenseInput, setAllowExpenseInput] = useState(false);
  const [allowInventoryInput, setAllowInventoryInput] = useState(false);
  const [refillByDate, setRefillByDate] = useState<Record<string, RefillEntry | null>>({});
  const [fixByDate, setFixByDate] = useState<Record<string, FixEntry | null>>({});
  const [fixOpenDate, setFixOpenDate] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const formatMoney = (value: number) => Number(value || 0).toFixed(0);
  const formatSnapshot = (snap?: InventorySnapshot | null): NormalizedSnapshot | null => {
    if (!snap) return null;
    return {
      full12: snap.full12 ?? 0,
      empty12: snap.empty12 ?? 0,
      total12: snap.total12 ?? (snap.full12 ?? 0) + (snap.empty12 ?? 0),
      full48: snap.full48 ?? 0,
      empty48: snap.empty48 ?? 0,
      total48: snap.total48 ?? (snap.full48 ?? 0) + (snap.empty48 ?? 0),
      as_of: snap.as_of,
      reason: snap.reason,
    };
  };
  const pricesQuery = usePriceSettings();
  const resolveBuyingPrice = useCallback(
    (gas: "12kg" | "48kg", date: string) => {
      const target = new Date(date);
      const prices = pricesQuery.data ?? [];
      const matches = prices.filter((p) => {
        if (p.gas_type !== gas) return false;
        if (p.customer_type !== "private" && p.customer_type !== "any") return false;
        if (!p.buying_price) return false;
        return new Date(p.effective_from) <= target;
      });
      matches.sort((a, b) => (a.effective_from < b.effective_from ? 1 : -1));
      return matches[0]?.buying_price ?? 0;
    },
    [pricesQuery.data]
  );
  const expenseTypes = ["fuel", "food", "car test", "car repair", "car insurance", "others"];
  const accessoryId = Platform.OS === "ios" ? "expenseAccessory" : undefined;
  const createRefill = useCreateRefill();
  const adjustInventory = useAdjustInventory();
  const refillsQuery = useInventoryRefills();
  const initialInventorySnapshot = useMemo(() => {
    if (!data || data.length === 0) return null;
    const oldest = data.reduce((acc, row) => (row.date < acc.date ? row : acc), data[0]);
    return formatSnapshot(oldest.inventory_start);
  }, [data]);
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!refillsQuery.data) return;
    const next: Record<string, RefillEntry | null> = {};
    refillsQuery.data.forEach((entry) => {
      next[entry.date] = {
        timeOfDay: entry.time_of_day,
        buy12: entry.buy12,
        ret12: entry.return12,
        buy48: entry.buy48,
        ret48: entry.return48,
      };
    });
    setRefillByDate(next);
  }, [refillsQuery.data]);
  useEffect(() => {
    if (viewMode === "inventory") {
      const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
      setAddShortcut({ mode: "inventory", date: today });
    }
  }, [viewMode]);
  const openInventoryShortcut = useCallback((date: string) => {
    setAddShortcut({ mode: "inventory", date });
    router.push("/(tabs)/add");
  }, []);

  const openExpenseModal = (date: string, preset?: { type: string; amount: number; note?: string | null }) => {
    setExpenseDate(date);
    if (preset) {
      const match = expenseTypes.includes(preset.type) ? preset.type : "";
      if (match) {
        setExpenseType(match);
        setUseCustomType(false);
        setCustomExpenseType("");
      } else {
        setUseCustomType(true);
        setCustomExpenseType(preset.type);
      }
      setExpenseAmount(String(preset.amount));
      setExpenseNote(preset.note ?? "");
    } else {
      setExpenseType("fuel");
      setCustomExpenseType("");
      setUseCustomType(false);
      setExpenseAmount("");
      setExpenseNote("");
    }
    setExpenseModalOpen(true);
  };

  const saveExpense = async () => {
    const date = expenseDate;
    const type = useCustomType ? customExpenseType.trim() : expenseType.trim();
    const amount = Number(expenseAmount);
    if (!date) return;
    if (!type) {
      Alert.alert("Missing type", "Please select or enter an expense type.");
      return;
    }
    if (!amount || amount <= 0) {
      Alert.alert("Invalid amount", "Please enter a valid amount.");
      return;
    }
    await createExpense.mutateAsync({
      date,
      expense_type: type,
      amount,
      note: expenseNote.trim() ? expenseNote.trim() : undefined,
    });
    setExpenseModalOpen(false);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    if (routeHandled) return;
    const mode = Array.isArray(params.mode) ? params.mode[0] : params.mode;
    const addExpense = Array.isArray(params.addExpense) ? params.addExpense[0] : params.addExpense;
    const expand = Array.isArray(params.expand) ? params.expand[0] : params.expand;
    const dateParam = Array.isArray(params.date) ? params.date[0] : params.date;
    const today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
    const date = dateParam || today;
    if (mode === "payments" || mode === "inventory") {
      setViewMode(mode);
    }
    if (addExpense === "1") {
      setAllowExpenseInput(true);
      setExpanded(date);
      openExpenseModal(date);
      setRouteHandled(true);
      return;
    }
    if (expand === "1") {
      setAllowInventoryInput(true);
      setExpanded(date);
      setRouteHandled(true);
    }
  }, [params, routeHandled]);

  useFocusEffect(
    useCallback(() => {
      refetch();
    }, [refetch])
  );

  const handleDeleteRefill = async (date: string, entry: RefillEntry) => {
    try {
      await createRefill.mutateAsync({
        date,
        time_of_day: entry.timeOfDay,
        buy12: -entry.buy12,
        return12: -entry.ret12,
        buy48: -entry.buy48,
        return48: -entry.ret48,
      });
      setRefillByDate((prev) => ({ ...prev, [date]: null }));
    } catch (err: any) {
      Alert.alert("Remove failed", err?.response?.data?.detail ?? "Failed to remove refill.");
    }
  };

  const handleDeleteFix = async (date: string, entry: FixEntry) => {
    try {
      if (entry.delta12.full || entry.delta12.empty) {
        await adjustInventory.mutateAsync({
          date,
          gas_type: "12kg",
          delta_full: -entry.delta12.full,
          delta_empty: -entry.delta12.empty,
          reason: "fix",
          note: "revert",
        });
      }
      if (entry.delta48.full || entry.delta48.empty) {
        await adjustInventory.mutateAsync({
          date,
          gas_type: "48kg",
          delta_full: -entry.delta48.full,
          delta_empty: -entry.delta48.empty,
          reason: "fix",
          note: "revert",
        });
      }
      setFixByDate((prev) => ({ ...prev, [date]: null }));
    } catch (err: any) {
      Alert.alert("Remove failed", err?.response?.data?.detail ?? "Failed to remove fix.");
    }
  };

  return (
    <View style={styles.container}>
      <Text style={styles.title}>Daily Reports</Text>
      <View style={styles.tabRow}>
        <Pressable
          onPress={() => setViewMode("payments")}
          style={[styles.tabChip, viewMode === "payments" && styles.tabChipActive]}
        >
          <Text style={[styles.tabChipText, viewMode === "payments" && styles.tabChipTextActive]}>Payments</Text>
        </Pressable>
        <Pressable
          onPress={() => setViewMode("inventory")}
          style={[styles.tabChip, viewMode === "inventory" && styles.tabChipActive]}
        >
          <Text style={[styles.tabChipText, viewMode === "inventory" && styles.tabChipTextActive]}>Inventory</Text>
        </Pressable>
      </View>
      {isLoading && <Text style={styles.meta}>Loading...</Text>}
      {error && <Text style={styles.error}>Failed to load reports.</Text>}
      <FlatList
        data={data ?? []}
        keyExtractor={(item) => item.date}
        ItemSeparatorComponent={() => <View style={{ height: 10 }} />}
        ListEmptyComponent={!isLoading ? <Text style={styles.meta}>No reports yet.</Text> : null}
        ListFooterComponent={
          viewMode === "inventory" && initialInventorySnapshot ? (
            <View style={{ marginTop: 10 }}>
              <View style={styles.labeledRowGroup}>
                <LabeledSection label="ini" color="#64748b">
                  <InventoryBlock title="" snapshot={initialInventorySnapshot} variant="grey" />
                </LabeledSection>
              </View>
            </View>
          ) : null
        }
        renderItem={({ item }) => {
          const unpaid = item.expected - item.received;
          const missing12 = Math.max(0, item.installed12 - item.received12);
          const missing48 = Math.max(0, item.installed48 - item.received48);
          const missingParts = [
            missing12 ? `12kg: ${missing12}` : null,
            missing48 ? `48kg: ${missing48}` : null,
          ].filter(Boolean) as string[];
          const missingTotal = missing12 + missing48;
          const orders = item.orders ?? [];
          const totalsByGas = (gas: "12kg" | "48kg") =>
            orders.reduce(
              (acc, order) => {
                const orderGas = (order as any).gas ?? (order as any).gas_type;
                if (orderGas !== gas) return acc;
                const total = (order as any).total ?? (order as any).price_total ?? 0;
                const paid = (order as any).paid ?? (order as any).paid_amount ?? 0;
                return { total: acc.total + total, paid: acc.paid + paid };
              },
              { total: 0, paid: 0 }
            );
          const totals12 = totalsByGas("12kg");
          const totals48 = totalsByGas("48kg");
          const startInv = formatSnapshot(item.inventory_start);
          const endInv = formatSnapshot(item.inventory_end);
          const refillEntry = refillByDate[item.date] ?? null;
          const fixEntry = fixByDate[item.date] ?? null;
          const buy12Price = resolveBuyingPrice("12kg", item.date);
          const buy48Price = resolveBuyingPrice("48kg", item.date);

          const isOpen = expanded === item.date;
          const weekday = new Date(item.date).toLocaleDateString("en-US", { weekday: "short" });
          return (
            <Pressable onPress={() => setExpanded(isOpen ? null : item.date)} style={({ pressed }) => [styles.card, pressed && styles.cardPressed]}>
              <View style={styles.rowBetween}>
                <View>
                  <View style={styles.dateRow}>
                    <Text style={styles.date}>
                      {weekday}, {item.display}
                    </Text>
                    {viewMode === "inventory" && (
                      <View style={styles.dayActions}>
                        <Pressable
                          onPress={() => openInventoryShortcut(item.date)}
                          style={styles.dayIconBtn}
                          accessibilityLabel="Add inventory"
                        >
                          <Ionicons name="add-circle-outline" size={18} color="#0a7ea4" />
                        </Pressable>
                        <Pressable
                          onPress={() => setFixOpenDate(item.date)}
                          style={styles.dayIconBtn}
                          accessibilityLabel="Add fix"
                        >
                          <Ionicons name="build-outline" size={18} color="#f97316" />
                        </Pressable>
                      </View>
                    )}
                  </View>
                  {viewMode === "payments" && (
                    <View style={styles.statusBelow}>
                      <View style={styles.statusRow}>
                        <Text style={[styles.statusText, styles.paid]}>Paid {formatMoney(item.received)}</Text>
                        {unpaid > 0 && (
                          <Text style={[styles.statusText, styles.unpaid]}> - Unpaid {formatMoney(unpaid)}</Text>
                        )}
                      </View>
                      <Text style={[styles.statusText, missingTotal > 0 ? styles.unpaid : styles.paid]}>
                        {missingTotal > 0 ? `Missing ${missingParts.join(" - ")}` : "Returned"}
                      </Text>
                    </View>
                  )}
                </View>
                {viewMode !== "payments" && (
                  <View style={{ alignItems: "flex-end" }}>
                    <View style={styles.statusRow}>
                      <Text style={[styles.statusText, styles.paid]}>Paid {formatMoney(item.received)}</Text>
                      {unpaid > 0 && (
                        <Text style={[styles.statusText, styles.unpaid]}> - Unpaid {formatMoney(unpaid)}</Text>
                      )}
                    </View>
                    <Text style={[styles.statusText, missingTotal > 0 ? styles.unpaid : styles.paid]}>
                      {missingTotal > 0 ? `Missing ${missingParts.join(" - ")}` : "Returned"}
                    </Text>
                  </View>
                )}
              </View>
              {viewMode === "payments" && (
                <View>
                  <View style={styles.labeledRowGroupCard}>
                    <LabeledSection label="sal" color="#0a7ea4">
                      <SalesTable
                        installed12={item.installed12}
                        received12={item.received12}
                        installed48={item.installed48}
                        received48={item.received48}
                        totals12={totals12}
                        totals48={totals48}
                        formatMoney={formatMoney}
                        showPayments={false}
                        showSigns={false}
                      />
                    </LabeledSection>
                    {isOpen && (
                      <View style={[styles.expanded, styles.labeledRowGroupCard]}>
                        <LabeledSection label="fix" color="#f97316">
                          <ExpenseSummary
                            date={item.date}
                            totalPaid={item.received}
                            formatMoney={formatMoney}
                            onEdit={(expense) => openExpenseModal(item.date, expense)}
                            onRemove={(expenseType) =>
                              deleteExpense.mutateAsync({ date: item.date, expense_type: expenseType })
                            }
                            allowAdd={allowExpenseInput}
                            onAdd={() => openExpenseModal(item.date)}
                          />
                        </LabeledSection>
                        <OrdersForDay date={item.date} orders={item.orders} />
                      </View>
                    )}
                  </View>
                </View>
              )}
              {viewMode === "inventory" && (
                <View>
                  {isOpen ? (
                    <View style={[styles.expanded, styles.labeledRowGroupCard]}>
                      <LabeledSection label="aft" color="#0f766e">
                        <InventoryBlock title="" snapshot={endInv} variant="grey" />
                      </LabeledSection>
                      <LabeledSection label="sal" color="#0a7ea4">
                        <SalesTable
                          installed12={item.installed12}
                          received12={item.received12}
                          installed48={item.installed48}
                          received48={item.received48}
                          totals12={totals12}
                          totals48={totals48}
                          formatMoney={formatMoney}
                          showPayments={false}
                          showSigns
                        />
                      </LabeledSection>
                      {fixEntry && (
                        <LabeledSection label="fix" color="#f97316">
                          <FixTable
                            entry={fixEntry}
                            onEdit={() => setFixOpenDate(item.date)}
                            onDelete={() => {
                              setFixOpenDate(null);
                              handleDeleteFix(
                                item.date,
                                fixEntry
                              );
                            }}
                          />
                        </LabeledSection>
                      )}
                      {refillEntry && (
                        <LabeledSection label="ref" color="#e0b93f">
                          <RefillTable
                            entry={refillEntry}
                            onEdit={() => openInventoryShortcut(item.date)}
                            onDelete={() => handleDeleteRefill(item.date, refillEntry)}
                          />
                        </LabeledSection>
                      )}
                      <LabeledSection label="bef" color="#64748b">
                        <InventoryBlock title="" snapshot={startInv} variant="grey" />
                      </LabeledSection>
                    </View>
                  ) : (
                    <View style={{ marginTop: 10 }}>
                      <View style={styles.labeledRowGroupCard}>
                        <LabeledSection label="sal" color="#0a7ea4">
                          <SalesTable
                            installed12={item.installed12}
                            received12={item.received12}
                            installed48={item.installed48}
                            received48={item.received48}
                            totals12={totals12}
                            totals48={totals48}
                            formatMoney={formatMoney}
                            showPayments={false}
                            showSigns={false}
                          />
                        </LabeledSection>
                      </View>
                    </View>
                  )}
                </View>
              )}
              {viewMode === "inventory" && (
                <FixModal
                  visible={fixOpenDate === item.date}
                  onClose={() => setFixOpenDate(null)}
                  date={item.date}
                  snapshot={endInv ?? startInv}
                  entry={fixEntry}
                  onSaved={(entry) => setFixByDate((prev) => ({ ...prev, [item.date]: entry }))}
                />
              )}
            </Pressable>
          );
        }}
      />
      <Modal visible={expenseModalOpen} transparent animationType="fade">
        <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
          <View style={styles.modalCard}>
            <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>Add expense</Text>
            <Text style={styles.modalMeta}>
              Date: {expenseDate ?? "-"}
            </Text>
            <Text style={styles.modalLabel}>Type</Text>
            <View style={styles.expenseChipRow}>
              {expenseTypes.map((type) => (
                <Pressable
                  key={type}
                  onPress={() => {
                    setExpenseType(type);
                    setUseCustomType(false);
                  }}
                  style={[styles.expenseChip, !useCustomType && expenseType === type && styles.expenseChipActive]}
                >
                  <Text style={[styles.expenseChipText, !useCustomType && expenseType === type && styles.expenseChipTextActive]}>
                    {type}
                  </Text>
                </Pressable>
              ))}
              <Pressable
                onPress={() => setUseCustomType(true)}
                style={[styles.expenseChip, useCustomType && styles.expenseChipActive]}
              >
                <Text style={[styles.expenseChipText, useCustomType && styles.expenseChipTextActive]}>Custom</Text>
              </Pressable>
            </View>
            {useCustomType && (
              <TextInput
                style={styles.modalInput}
                placeholder="Enter expense type"
                value={customExpenseType}
                onChangeText={setCustomExpenseType}
                returnKeyType="done"
                blurOnSubmit
                onSubmitEditing={() => Keyboard.dismiss()}
                inputAccessoryViewID={accessoryId}
              />
            )}
            <Text style={styles.modalLabel}>Amount</Text>
            <TextInput
              style={styles.modalInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={expenseAmount}
              onChangeText={setExpenseAmount}
              returnKeyType="done"
              blurOnSubmit
              onSubmitEditing={() => Keyboard.dismiss()}
              inputAccessoryViewID={accessoryId}
            />
            <Text style={styles.modalLabel}>Note (optional)</Text>
            <TextInput
              style={[styles.modalInput, styles.modalInputNote]}
              placeholder="Add a note"
              value={expenseNote}
              onChangeText={setExpenseNote}
              multiline
              returnKeyType="done"
              blurOnSubmit
              onSubmitEditing={() => Keyboard.dismiss()}
              inputAccessoryViewID={accessoryId}
            />
            <View style={styles.expenseActions}>
              <Pressable style={styles.expenseCancel} onPress={() => setExpenseModalOpen(false)}>
                <Text style={styles.expenseCancelText}>Cancel</Text>
              </Pressable>
              <Pressable style={styles.expenseSave} onPress={saveExpense}>
                <Text style={styles.expenseSaveText}>Save</Text>
              </Pressable>
            </View>
          </View>
        </View>
      </Modal>
      {Platform.OS === "ios" && (
        <InputAccessoryView nativeID={accessoryId}>
          <View style={styles.accessoryRow}>
            <Pressable onPress={() => Keyboard.dismiss()} style={styles.accessoryButton}>
              <Text style={styles.accessoryText}>Done</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
        </InputAccessoryView>
      )}
    </View>
  );
}

function OrdersForDay({ date, orders }: { date: string; orders?: DailyReportRow["orders"] }) {
  const shouldFetch = !orders || orders.length === 0;
  const { data, isLoading, error } = useOrdersByDay(shouldFetch ? date : undefined);
  const list = orders ?? data ?? [];
  return (
    <View style={styles.sectionBlock}>
      <Text style={styles.expandedTitle}>Orders</Text>
      {shouldFetch && isLoading && <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>Loading...</Text>}
      {error && shouldFetch && <Text style={[styles.orderMeta, styles.unpaid]}>Failed to load.</Text>}
      {list.map((order) => {
        // Support enriched shape from daily reports or raw orders
        const name = (order as any).customer ?? (order as any).id;
        const system = (order as any).system ?? (order as any).system_id ?? "";
        const customerNotes =
          (order as any).note ??
          (order as any).customer_notes ??
          (order as any).customer_description ??
          (order as any).customer_details ??
          "";
        const gas = (order as any).gas ?? (order as any).gas_type;
        const installed = (order as any).installed ?? (order as any).cylinders_installed;
        const received = (order as any).receivedCyl ?? (order as any).cylinders_received;
        const total = (order as any).total ?? (order as any).price_total;
        const paid = (order as any).paid ?? (order as any).paid_amount;
        const orderUnpaid = (total || 0) - (paid || 0);
        const unreturned = (installed || 0) - (received || 0);
        const receivedLow = (received || 0) < (installed || 0);
        const underpaid = (paid || 0) < (total || 0);

        return (
          <View key={order.id} style={styles.orderRow}>
            <View>
              <Text style={styles.orderName}>{name}</Text>
              {customerNotes ? <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>{customerNotes}</Text> : null}
              <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>
                {gas} - {system}
              </Text>
              <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>
                Installed <Text style={receivedLow ? styles.unpaid : undefined}>{installed}</Text> - Received{" "}
                <Text style={receivedLow ? styles.unpaid : undefined}>{received}</Text>
              </Text>
              <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>
                Total {total} - Paid <Text style={underpaid ? styles.unpaid : undefined}>{paid}</Text>
              </Text>
            </View>
            <View style={{ alignItems: "flex-end" }}>
              <Text style={[styles.orderStatus, orderUnpaid > 0 ? styles.unpaid : styles.paid]}>
                {orderUnpaid > 0 ? `Unpaid ${orderUnpaid}` : "Paid"}
              </Text>
              <Text style={[styles.orderStatus, unreturned > 0 ? styles.unpaid : styles.paid]}>
                {unreturned > 0 ? `${unreturned} unreturned` : "Returned"}
              </Text>
            </View>
          </View>
        );
      })}
      {list.length === 0 && !isLoading && <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>No orders for this day.</Text>}
    </View>
  );
}

function ExpenseSummary({
  date,
  totalPaid,
  formatMoney,
  onEdit,
  onRemove,
  allowAdd,
  onAdd,
}: {
  date: string;
  totalPaid: number;
  formatMoney: (value: number) => string;
  onEdit: (expense: { type: string; amount: number; note?: string | null }) => void;
  onRemove: (expenseType: string) => void;
  allowAdd: boolean;
  onAdd: () => void;
}) {
  const { data, isLoading } = useExpenses(date, { enabled: !!date });
  if (isLoading) {
    return <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>Loading expenses...</Text>;
  }
  if (!data || data.length === 0) {
    return allowAdd ? (
      <Pressable onPress={onAdd} style={styles.inlineAdd}>
        <Text style={styles.inlineAddText}>+ Add expense</Text>
      </Pressable>
    ) : null;
  }
  const total = data.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.amount || 0), 0);
  const netPaid = totalPaid - total;
  return (
    <View>
      <View style={styles.expenseRow}>
        <Text style={styles.expenseLabel}>Net collected</Text>
          <View style={styles.expenseRight}>
            <Text style={styles.expenseValue}>{formatMoney(netPaid)}</Text>
          </View>
        </View>
      {data.map((item) => (
        <View key={`${item.date}-${item.expense_type}`} style={styles.expenseRow}>
          <Text style={styles.expenseLabel}>{item.expense_type}</Text>
          <View style={styles.expenseRight}>
            {allowAdd && (
              <Pressable onPress={() => onEdit({ type: item.expense_type, amount: item.amount, note: item.note })}>
                <Ionicons name="create-outline" size={16} color="#0a7ea4" />
              </Pressable>
            )}
            {allowAdd && (
              <Pressable onPress={() => onRemove(item.expense_type)}>
                <Ionicons name="trash-outline" size={16} color="#b00020" />
              </Pressable>
            )}
            <Text style={styles.expenseValue}>-{formatMoney(item.amount)}</Text>
          </View>
        </View>
      ))}
      <View style={styles.expenseRow}>
        <Text style={styles.expenseLabel}>Total paid</Text>
        <View style={styles.expenseRight}>
          <Text style={styles.expenseValue}>{formatMoney(totalPaid)}</Text>
        </View>
      </View>
      {allowAdd && (
        <Pressable onPress={onAdd} style={styles.inlineAdd}>
          <Text style={styles.inlineAddText}>+ Add expense</Text>
        </Pressable>
      )}
    </View>
  );
}

type GasTotals = { total: number; paid: number };

function SalesTable({
  installed12,
  received12,
  installed48,
  received48,
  totals12,
  totals48,
  formatMoney,
  showPayments = true,
  showSigns = true,
}: {
  installed12: number;
  received12: number;
  installed48: number;
  received48: number;
  totals12: GasTotals;
  totals48: GasTotals;
  formatMoney: (value: number) => string;
  showPayments?: boolean;
  showSigns?: boolean;
}) {
  if (!showPayments) {
    const installed12Text = showSigns ? `-${installed12}` : `${installed12}`;
    const received12Text = showSigns ? `+${received12}` : `${received12}`;
    const installed48Text = showSigns ? `-${installed48}` : `${installed48}`;
    const received48Text = showSigns ? `+${received48}` : `${received48}`;
    return (
      <View style={styles.salesTable}>
        <View style={[styles.tableRow, styles.salesHeader]}>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.salesHeadText]}>Installed 12kg</Text>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.salesHeadText]}>Received 12kg</Text>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.salesHeadText]}>Installed 48kg</Text>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.salesHeadText]}>Received 48kg</Text>
        </View>
        <View style={styles.tableRow}>
          <Text style={styles.salesCell}>{installed12Text}</Text>
          <Text style={styles.salesCell}>{received12Text}</Text>
          <Text style={styles.salesCell}>{installed48Text}</Text>
          <Text style={styles.salesCell}>{received48Text}</Text>
        </View>
      </View>
    );
  }
  return (
    <View style={styles.table}>
      <View style={[styles.tableRow, styles.tableHeader]}>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableHeadText]}>Gas</Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableHeadText]}>Installed</Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableHeadText]}>Received</Text>
        {showPayments && <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableHeadText]}>Total</Text>}
        {showPayments && <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableHeadText]}>Paid</Text>}
      </View>
      <View style={styles.tableRow}>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableLabel]}>12kg</Text>
        <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{installed12}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{received12}</Text>
        {showPayments && <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{formatMoney(totals12.total)}</Text>}
        {showPayments && <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{formatMoney(totals12.paid)}</Text>}
      </View>
      <View style={styles.tableRow}>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.tableLabel]}>48kg</Text>
        <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{installed48}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{received48}</Text>
        {showPayments && <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{formatMoney(totals48.total)}</Text>}
        {showPayments && <Text style={styles.tableCell}>{formatMoney(totals48.paid)}</Text>}
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

function RefillTable({
  entry,
  onEdit,
  onDelete,
}: {
  entry: RefillEntry;
  onEdit: () => void;
  onDelete: () => void;
}) {
  return (
    <View style={styles.inventoryGreyTable}>
      <View style={[styles.tableRow, styles.inventoryGreyHeader]}>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]} numberOfLines={1}>
          Buy 12
        </Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]} numberOfLines={1}>
          Ret 12
        </Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]} numberOfLines={1}>
          Buy 48
        </Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]} numberOfLines={1}>
          Ret 48
        </Text>
      </View>
      <View style={styles.tableRow}>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>+{entry.buy12}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>-{entry.ret12}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>+{entry.buy48}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>-{entry.ret48}</Text>
      </View>
      <View style={styles.refillActionsTop}>
        <Pressable style={styles.refillIconButton} onPress={onEdit}>
          <Ionicons name="build-outline" size={14} color="#0a7ea4" />
        </Pressable>
        <Pressable style={styles.refillIconButton} onPress={onDelete}>
          <Ionicons name="trash-outline" size={14} color="#b00020" />
        </Pressable>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

function RefillModal({
  visible,
  onClose,
  date,
  startSnapshot,
  endSnapshot,
  entry,
  buy12Price,
  buy48Price,
  onSaved,
}: {
  visible: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  date: string;
  startSnapshot: NormalizedSnapshot | null;
  endSnapshot: NormalizedSnapshot | null;
  entry: RefillEntry | null;
  buy12Price: number;
  buy48Price: number;
  onSaved: (entry: RefillEntry) => void;
}) {
  const [timeOfDay, setTimeOfDay] = useState<"morning" | "evening">("morning");
  const [buy12, setBuy12] = useState("");
  const [ret12, setRet12] = useState("");
  const [buy48, setBuy48] = useState("");
  const [ret48, setRet48] = useState("");
  const createRefill = useCreateRefill();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!visible) return;
    setTimeOfDay(entry?.timeOfDay ?? "morning");
    setBuy12(entry ? String(entry.buy12) : "");
    setRet12(entry ? String(entry.ret12) : "");
    setBuy48(entry ? String(entry.buy48) : "");
    setRet48(entry ? String(entry.ret48) : "");
  }, [visible, entry]);

  const snapshot = timeOfDay === "morning" ? startSnapshot : endSnapshot;
  const cost =
    (Number(buy12) || 0) * (buy12Price || 0) + (Number(buy48) || 0) * (buy48Price || 0);

  const onSave = async () => {
    if (!snapshot) {
      Alert.alert("Missing inventory", `No ${timeOfDay} inventory available for this day.`);
      return;
    }
    const r12 = Number(ret12) || 0;
    const r48 = Number(ret48) || 0;
    const b12 = Number(buy12) || 0;
    const b48 = Number(buy48) || 0;
    if (r12 > snapshot.empty12) {
      Alert.alert("Invalid return", "12kg returning cannot exceed available empty 12kg cylinders.");
      return;
    }
    if (r48 > snapshot.empty48) {
      Alert.alert("Invalid return", "48kg returning cannot exceed available empty 48kg cylinders.");
      return;
    }
    const nextEntry: RefillEntry = { timeOfDay, buy12: b12, ret12: r12, buy48: b48, ret48: r48 };
    try {
      if (entry) {
        if (entry.timeOfDay !== timeOfDay) {
          await createRefill.mutateAsync({
            date,
            time_of_day: entry.timeOfDay,
            buy12: -entry.buy12,
            return12: -entry.ret12,
            buy48: -entry.buy48,
            return48: -entry.ret48,
          });
          await createRefill.mutateAsync({
            date,
            time_of_day: timeOfDay,
            buy12: b12,
            return12: r12,
            buy48: b48,
            return48: r48,
          });
        } else {
          await createRefill.mutateAsync({
            date,
            time_of_day: timeOfDay,
            buy12: b12 - entry.buy12,
            return12: r12 - entry.ret12,
            buy48: b48 - entry.buy48,
            return48: r48 - entry.ret48,
          });
        }
      } else {
        await createRefill.mutateAsync({
          date,
          time_of_day: timeOfDay,
          buy12: b12,
          return12: r12,
          buy48: b48,
          return48: r48,
        });
      }
      onSaved(nextEntry);
      onClose();
    } catch (err: any) {
      Alert.alert("Refill failed", err?.response?.data?.detail ?? "Failed to save refill.");
    }
  };

  return (
    <Modal visible={visible} transparent animationType="fade" onRequestClose={onClose}>
      <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
        <View style={styles.modalCard}>
          <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>{entry ? "Update refill" : "Add refill"}</Text>
          <View style={styles.timeToggle}>
            <Pressable
              style={[styles.timeChip, timeOfDay === "morning" && styles.timeChipActive]}
              onPress={() => setTimeOfDay("morning")}
            >
              <Text style={[styles.timeChipText, timeOfDay === "morning" && styles.timeChipTextActive]}>Morning</Text>
            </Pressable>
            <Pressable
              style={[styles.timeChip, timeOfDay === "evening" && styles.timeChipActive]}
              onPress={() => setTimeOfDay("evening")}
            >
              <Text style={[styles.timeChipText, timeOfDay === "evening" && styles.timeChipTextActive]}>Evening</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
          {snapshot ? (
            <Text style={styles.refillMeta}>
              Inventory: 12kg Full {snapshot.full12} - Empty {snapshot.empty12} - 48kg Full {snapshot.full48} - Empty {snapshot.empty48}
            </Text>
          ) : (
            <Text style={[styles.refillMeta, styles.unpaid]}>No inventory snapshot for this time.</Text>
          )}
          <View style={[styles.tableRow, styles.refillHeader]}>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>Buy 12kg</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>Ret 12kg</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>Buy 48kg</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>Ret 48kg</Text>
          </View>
          <View style={styles.tableRow}>
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={buy12}
              onChangeText={setBuy12}
              editable
              selectTextOnFocus
            />
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={ret12}
              onChangeText={setRet12}
              editable
              selectTextOnFocus
            />
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={buy48}
              onChangeText={setBuy48}
              editable
              selectTextOnFocus
            />
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={ret48}
              onChangeText={setRet48}
              editable
              selectTextOnFocus
            />
          </View>
          <Text style={styles.refillMeta}>
            Distributor cost: {Number.isNaN(cost) ? "0" : cost.toFixed(0)}
          </Text>
          <View style={styles.refillActions}>
            <Pressable style={styles.refillClear} onPress={() => {
              setBuy12("");
              setRet12("");
              setBuy48("");
              setRet48("");
            }}>
              <Text style={styles.refillClearText}>Clear</Text>
            </Pressable>
            <Pressable style={styles.refillSave} onPress={onSave}>
              <Text style={styles.refillSaveText}>Save</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
          <Pressable style={styles.modalClose} onPress={onClose}>
            <Text style={styles.modalCloseText}>Close</Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
      </View>
    </Modal>
  );
}

function FixTable({
  entry,
  onEdit,
  onDelete,
}: {
  entry: FixEntry;
  onEdit: () => void;
  onDelete: () => void;
}) {
  return (
    <View style={styles.inventoryGreyTable}>
      <View style={[styles.tableRow, styles.inventoryGreyHeader]}>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]}>12kg Full</Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]}>12kg Empty</Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]}>48kg Full</Text>
        <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.inventoryGreyHeadText]}>48kg Empty</Text>
      </View>
      <View style={styles.tableRow}>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>{entry.full12}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>{entry.empty12}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>{entry.full48}</Text>
        <Text style={styles.inventoryGreyCell}>{entry.empty48}</Text>
      </View>
      <Text style={styles.fixReasonText}>Reason: {entry.reason}</Text>
      {entry.note ? <Text style={styles.fixReasonText}>Note: {entry.note}</Text> : null}
      <View style={styles.refillActionsTop}>
        <Pressable style={styles.refillIconButton} onPress={onEdit}>
          <Ionicons name="build-outline" size={14} color="#0a7ea4" />
        </Pressable>
        <Pressable style={styles.refillIconButton} onPress={onDelete}>
          <Ionicons name="trash-outline" size={14} color="#b00020" />
        </Pressable>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

function FixModal({
  visible,
  onClose,
  date,
  snapshot,
  entry,
  onSaved,
}: {
  visible: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  date: string;
  snapshot: NormalizedSnapshot | null;
  entry: FixEntry | null;
  onSaved: (entry: FixEntry) => void;
}) {
  const [full12, setFull12] = useState("");
  const [empty12, setEmpty12] = useState("");
  const [full48, setFull48] = useState("");
  const [empty48, setEmpty48] = useState("");
  const [reason, setReason] = useState("unknown");
  const [note, setNote] = useState("");
  const adjustInventory = useAdjustInventory();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!visible) return;
    const base = entry ?? snapshot;
    if (base) {
      setFull12(String(base.full12));
      setEmpty12(String(base.empty12));
      setFull48(String(base.full48));
      setEmpty48(String(base.empty48));
    } else {
      setFull12("");
      setEmpty12("");
      setFull48("");
      setEmpty48("");
    }
    setReason(entry?.reason ?? "unknown");
    setNote(entry?.note ?? "");
  }, [visible, entry, snapshot]);

  const onSave = async () => {
    if (!snapshot) {
      Alert.alert("Missing inventory", "No inventory snapshot available for this day.");
      return;
    }
    const nextFull12 = Number(full12) || 0;
    const nextEmpty12 = Number(empty12) || 0;
    const nextFull48 = Number(full48) || 0;
    const nextEmpty48 = Number(empty48) || 0;
    const delta12 = {
      full: nextFull12 - snapshot.full12,
      empty: nextEmpty12 - snapshot.empty12,
    };
    const delta48 = {
      full: nextFull48 - snapshot.full48,
      empty: nextEmpty48 - snapshot.empty48,
    };
    if (!delta12.full && !delta12.empty && !delta48.full && !delta48.empty) {
      Alert.alert("No changes", "Update at least one value.");
      return;
    }
    try {
      if (delta12.full || delta12.empty) {
        await adjustInventory.mutateAsync({
          date,
          gas_type: "12kg",
          delta_full: delta12.full,
          delta_empty: delta12.empty,
          reason,
          note: note.trim() ? note.trim() : undefined,
        });
      }
      if (delta48.full || delta48.empty) {
        await adjustInventory.mutateAsync({
          date,
          gas_type: "48kg",
          delta_full: delta48.full,
          delta_empty: delta48.empty,
          reason,
          note: note.trim() ? note.trim() : undefined,
        });
      }
      onSaved({
        full12: nextFull12,
        empty12: nextEmpty12,
        full48: nextFull48,
        empty48: nextEmpty48,
        reason,
        note: note.trim() ? note.trim() : undefined,
        delta12,
        delta48,
      });
      onClose();
    } catch (err: any) {
      Alert.alert("Fix failed", err?.response?.data?.detail ?? "Failed to save fix.");
    }
  };

  const reasonOptions = ["buy", "sold", "lost", "gained", "unknown", "else"];

  return (
    <Modal visible={visible} transparent animationType="fade" onRequestClose={onClose}>
      <View style={styles.modalOverlay}>
        <View style={styles.modalCard}>
          <Text style={styles.modalTitle}>{entry ? "Update fix" : "Add fix"}</Text>
          {snapshot ? (
            <Text style={styles.refillMeta}>
              Current: 12kg Full {snapshot.full12} - Empty {snapshot.empty12} - 48kg Full {snapshot.full48} - Empty {snapshot.empty48}
            </Text>
          ) : (
            <Text style={[styles.refillMeta, styles.unpaid]}>No inventory snapshot for this day.</Text>
          )}
          <View style={[styles.tableRow, styles.refillHeader]}>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>New 12kg Full</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>New 12kg Empty</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>New 48kg Full</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tableCell, styles.refillHeadText]}>New 48kg Empty</Text>
          </View>
          <View style={styles.tableRow}>
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={full12}
              onChangeText={setFull12}
            />
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={empty12}
              onChangeText={setEmpty12}
            />
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={full48}
              onChangeText={setFull48}
            />
            <TextInput
              style={styles.refillInput}
              keyboardType="numeric"
              inputMode="numeric"
              placeholder="0"
              value={empty48}
              onChangeText={setEmpty48}
            />
          </View>
          <Text style={styles.modalLabel}>Reason</Text>
          <View style={styles.expenseChipRow}>
            {reasonOptions.map((option) => (
              <Pressable
                key={option}
                onPress={() => setReason(option)}
                style={[styles.expenseChip, reason === option && styles.expenseChipActive]}
              >
                <Text style={[styles.expenseChipText, reason === option && styles.expenseChipTextActive]}>
                  {option}
                </Text>
              </Pressable>
            ))}
          </View>
          <Text style={styles.modalLabel}>Notes</Text>
          <TextInput
            style={[styles.modalInput, styles.modalInputNote]}
            placeholder="Add a note"
            value={note}
            onChangeText={setNote}
            multiline
          />
          <View style={styles.refillActions}>
            <Pressable style={styles.refillClear} onPress={() => {
              setFull12("");
              setEmpty12("");
              setFull48("");
              setEmpty48("");
            }}>
              <Text style={styles.refillClearText}>Clear</Text>
            </Pressable>
            <Pressable style={styles.refillSave} onPress={onSave}>
              <Text style={styles.refillSaveText}>Save</Text>
            </Pressable>
          </View>
          <Pressable style={styles.modalClose} onPress={onClose}>
            <Text style={styles.modalCloseText}>Close</Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
      </View>
    </Modal>
  );
}

function InventoryBlock({
  title,
  snapshot,
  variant = "default",
}: {
  title: string;
  snapshot: NormalizedSnapshot | null;
  variant?: "default" | "grey";
}) {
  if (!snapshot) {
    return (
      <View style={styles.sectionBlock}>
        {title ? <Text style={styles.expandedTitle}>{title}</Text> : null}
        <Text style={styles.orderMeta}>No inventory snapshot.</Text>
      </View>
    );
  }
  return (
    <View style={styles.sectionBlock}>
      {title ? <Text style={styles.expandedTitle}>{title}</Text> : null}
      <View style={variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyTable : styles.salesTable}>
        <View style={[styles.tableRow, variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyHeader : styles.salesHeader]}>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyHeadText : styles.salesHeadText]}>12kg Full</Text>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyHeadText : styles.salesHeadText]}>12kg Empty</Text>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyHeadText : styles.salesHeadText]}>48kg Full</Text>
          <Text style={[styles.tableCell, variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyHeadText : styles.salesHeadText]}>48kg Empty</Text>
        </View>
        <View style={styles.tableRow}>
          <Text style={variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyCell : styles.salesCell}>{snapshot.full12}</Text>
          <Text style={variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyCell : styles.salesCell}>{snapshot.empty12}</Text>
          <Text style={variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyCell : styles.salesCell}>{snapshot.full48}</Text>
          <Text style={variant === "grey" ? styles.inventoryGreyCell : styles.salesCell}>{snapshot.empty48}</Text>
        </View>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

function LabeledSection({
  label,
  color,
  children,
}: {
  label: string;
  color: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <View style={styles.labeledRow}>
      <View style={[styles.labeledTag, { backgroundColor: color }]}>
        <Text style={styles.labeledTagText} numberOfLines={1}>
          {label}
        </Text>
      </View>
      <View style={styles.labeledContent}>{children}</View>
    </View>
  );
}
